    fun shape ->

        | Cube(s) => s ** 3.0

type Radius = Float in
type SideLength = Float in
type Height = Float in

type Shape =
  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

let volume : Shape -> Float =
    fun shape ->
        case shape
        | Sphere(r) => 4.0 / 3.0 * pi * r ** 3.0
        | Cube(s) => s ** 3.0
        | Cylinder(r, h) => pi * r ** 2.0 * h end in
